saturninus thou knoweſt great loue haue borne thee many good deedes haue done thee thy houſe wherof needeth token beholding thee ſo highly aduaunced court ſo accepted ſeruice many offended thee al men haue enuie friend parent acquaintance recommended ſeruaunts whome haue done vnto ſome much beholding others haue cō ſidered ſeruice theſe notwithſtanding thee onely fixed mine eye magnifie thee thee imployed hart loue thee ſent thee recompt vnto thee trauels ſorrowes end thou ſhouldeſt helpe deliuer mee herein thou ſhalt perceiue affectionate loue beare thee repoſe confidence thee wherein would truſt mine owne proper ſonne ſonnes thincke howe inherite father good verie friendes haue care deliuer friendes griefe ſorrowe thou well knoweſt saturninus great ſeruice haue done seuerus ſince youth haue followed warres ſay ſerued ſo young alone moſt auncient ſeruaunt although bee moſt forgotten abhorred setting part ſeruices haue done great daungers haue paſſed deliuer perill haue borne ſo tender affection vnto lord seuerus left like man adore god true appeareth moſt cleare gaue daughter vnto ſonne baſſianus ſelfe perpetuall ſlaue ſpent youth ſeruice followed father throughout world
